The dealer deals five cards face down, and one at a time to each player in a clockwise direction. The rest of the cards are stacked and kept in the center as the draw pile. The topmost card is placed face up to initiate the discard pile, next to the draw pile. \r\n\r\nPlay with your friends, against the computer, against millions of Tonk players around the world.\r\n\r\nYou can also create Private Rooms and invite your friends to play.\r\n\r\nIt is an enjoyable card game that is both fast-paced and strategic.\r\n\r\nPlay this classic card game with your friends or against real players from anywhere in the world.\r\n\r\nYou might have played many card games but there is nothing like Tonk.\r\n\r\nGive our game a try.
